The LutiKey app is supported in the following languages: English, Spanish, Portuguese, Chinese, Dutch, French, German, Italian, Japanese, Korean and Russian Is LutiKey waterproof? Yes. Lutikey is waterproof IP67. How long does Lutikey’s battery last? The Lutikey’s battery is  to last one full year. Is it possible to replace the LutiKey battery? Yes, the LutiKey battery is replaceable. How many LutiKeys can be managed by one device? One Lutikey app can manage unlimited Lutikey devices at the same time. Is my information maintained privately? Your information will be kept completely safe and anonymous and will always be protected. LutiKey does not share your information with anyone at any time. The only time someone can see your information is if you share your LutiKey with that person. Could I transfer a used LutiKey to another person? Yes. First, remove the Lutikey from your App while it is connected. Once the Lutikey App notices that it is no longer connected with your previous device, it may be transferred. How Does LutiKey Work? Lutikey works through Bluetooth connection. The location is reported to the phone through this connection. Once the connection is determined both the phone and the device will give a lost alert signal. Bluetooth has a high frequency band, which effectiveness for communication maybe limited by the environment. Multiple walls, solid objects, and other interferences may decrease the effectiveness of the Bluetooth signal. We have maximized the Lutikey range for personal item tracking within normal distance. What is the LutiKey community? Once you have reported that your Lutikey is lost, the information will be distributed to the Lutikey cloud service. This information will then be passed safely to all connected devices that have joined the community. When another device in the community has detected the signal of the lost Lutikey, this information will be reported back to the cloud service and in turn to you. Do I have to own a LutiKey device to belong to the LutiKey Community? Lutikey welcomes everyone whether they own a LutiKey device or not. The Lutikey App is free to download and by doing so, you’ll be joining a growing community that will always help find your lost items. All you need to do is download the app and create an account and you’ll also be able to help others find their lost items too. Does LutiKey requires a paid subscription? Absolutely not! Even though we recommend everyone to take full advantage of all the functionalities that are offered on our Plus and Premium subscriptions, when you connect your LutiKey with your phone, you’ll have full access to all functions that the LutiKey App has to offer on its basic plan, including our growing community.
